                <tr>
                    <td style="background-color: #FFF; padding-bottom: 5px;"
                        valign="top">

                        <span style="padding-left: 5px;">
                            <strong style="font-size:15pt;">Erasmo Ramirez</strong></span>
                        <div class="spacer_10"></div>
                        <div style="font-size: 10pt; padding-left: 5px;">
                            <strong>Birthdate:</strong> 5/2/1990 (27 y, 2 m, 30 d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>Bats/Throws:</strong> R/R &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>Height/Weight:</strong> 5-11/200 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>Position:</strong> P<br /><strong>Contract:</strong> <a href="statss.aspx?playerid=10314&position=P#contract" style="text-decoration:none;">$3.1M / 1 Years (2017)</a>
                        </div>
                    </td>
                    
                    <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-top:5px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px;"><b><a href="http://www.rotowire.com/users/ad_jump.asp?id=688&playerid=12117" style="text-decoration:none;">RotoWire News</a>:</b> Ramirez will slot into the Mariners' rotation, beginning Tuesday against the Rangers, Greg Johns of MLB.com reports. (7/28/2017)</div></td></tr>

                </tr>
                <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; vertical-align:top; padding-bottom:4px; padding-left:5px;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:13pt"><span class="m_date">9/21/2016</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/erasmo-ramirez-super-reliever/">Erasmo Ramirez, Super-Reliever</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/index.php?author=43631">August Fagerstrom (FanGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/erasmo-ramirez-super-reliever/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />5</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">6/29/2016</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-360-rockiescorner/">The Sleeper and the Bust Episode: 360 – #RockiesCo&raquo;</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=11752">Paul Sporer (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-360-rockiescorner/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />3</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">3/8/2016</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/rays-playing-time-battles-pitchers/">Rays Playing Time Battles: Pitchers</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=34468">Blake Murphy (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/rays-playing-time-battles-pitchers/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />0</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">1/19/2016</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-change-strikeouts-minus-walks-but-with-popups/">The Change: Strikeouts Minus Walks, But With Popup&raquo;</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=22">Eno Sarris (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-change-strikeouts-minus-walks-but-with-popups/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />14</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">10/13/2015</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-roto-deep-league-cy-young/">The Roto Deep League Cy Young</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=22">Eno Sarris (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-roto-deep-league-cy-young/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />8</a></span><br /></div></td></tr>

                <tr id="so1" style="background-color: #FFF;"><td colspan="5" style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="width:100%; font-size:10pt"><center>Profiles:&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa5" href="javascript:showMoreSO2013();">2013</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa6" href="javascript:showMoreSO2014();">2014</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa7" href="javascript:showMoreSO2015();">2015</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa8" href="javascript:showMoreSO2016();">2016</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa9"  href="javascript:showMoreSO2017();">2017</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;(Click Year to Expand / <a href="javascript:hideSO('so1');">Close</a>)</center></div></td></tr>
                
                
                
                <tr id="so5" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Erasmo Ramirez might not be tall in stature, but he's got some big stuff. He consistently sits in the 93 mph range, but can touch 95 and he has thing of beauty for a change up. As a starter in 2012, Ramirez had a 3.64 ERA with a 0.98 whip striking out 22% of opposing batters, walking only 4%, and holding opponents to a .218/.247/.362 slash line.  Ramirez won't be a world beater, but he's a sneaky late round or inexpensive grab for favorable match-ups. His minor league numbers don't suggest much in the way of upside in strikeouts, but he's probably a safe bet for a 20% K rate, an ERA around 3.60 and a WHIP somewhere in the 1.12 range. His terrific control and home park (despite the fences moving in a bit) should certainly help his overall stat line, although wins might be tough to come by for Mariner starters in 2013. <a href="”https://twitter.com/michaelcbarr”"> (<a href="https://twitter.com/michaelcbarr">Michael Barr</a>) </a><br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Not to be mistaken for the "other" Erasmo Ramirez, this Erasmo has one of the game's better out pitches in his change-up and he can bring plus heat when needed. Ramirez is a control expert too, which contributed to his 0.98 WHIP as a starter in 2012. Certainly not a candidate to anchor your staff, Ramirez is a nice starter to have around either as your #5 or frequent spot starter for favorable match-ups. There's also some potential that he could turn into something more, and at just 22 years of age, he's a good dynasty league stash.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so6" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>It's kind of hard to believe that Erasmo Ramirez's season didn't get off the ground until mid-season because of Jeremy Bonderman and Aaron Harang, but that's pretty much what happened in 2013. Starting the season on the disabled list, and then languishing in Triple-A until the roof caved in, Ramirez finally got his shot in the rotation in July, and the results weren't quite what some of the craftier starting pitching mavens were hoping for out of the 23-year-old. Ramirez was inconsistent, struggling with his control where that was once one of his signature strengths. He induced fewer swings outside the strike zone in 2013 and when batters swung, they made 11% more contact than the year prior. His swinging strike rate was a far more human 8.8% vs. 11.3% the year prior and in general he appeared to be a pretty average pitcher. His role in 2014 is still yet undefined. (Michael Barr)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>An injury, a lost tick on the fastball, and suddenly Erasmo Ramirez looked a lot more human in 2013. Right now, he's probably a factor in the Seattle rotation, but his odds of being a factor in your fantasy rotation obviously got a lot longer.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so7" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Now that Erasmo Ramirez has 200+ innings spread out over three seasons, now that his team no longer has a big league rotation spot reserved for him, now that he's shown serious home run issues in every season, now that he's really been above-average only once and that was three years ago, now that that velocity boost that made him interesting has subsided and left him with below-average velocity -- now we can finally stop thinking about Erasmo Ramirez, right? Here's the weird thing. Last year, in a year that saw Ramirez put his worst results by traditional numbers (5.26 ERA) and peripherals (17.8% strikeout rate, 10.1% walk rate, 37.7% ground-ball rate), Ramirez still had a solid arsenal. His four-seamer, slider, change, and curve all had average or above-average whiff rates. So there's still a little bit of hope. It's now just reserved for the dreamers like us, plugging away in deep leagues and wondering what warm body we should put on our AL-only bench, and what name hasn't been combed over by an industry that combs every hair over the bald spot that is our pitching budget. (Eno Sarris)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Once you get to the bottom of your sleepers list, maybe make some room for Erasmo Ramirez. Sure, those high fastballs have lead to homers, and his command is spotty, and his pitches aren't always all there at the same time, and he doesn't have a starting role right now. If you zoom out, he's still only 24 and he still has four major league pitches.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so8" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>The changeup has always been great, so Erasmo Ramirez always had a chance to make it in the big leagues. But the velocity that popped up and made him a super sleeper has gone. And the above-average whiff rates on his breaking pitches have always hidden the bad ball in play numbers -- he can't command those breakers well, and so he gives up home runs on them. The Mariners gave him some chances, but maybe never a real long look, and then basically gave him away to the Rays. Then the Rays told him to use his slider as a show-me pitch, a strike-stealing pitch, and everything started to work together. Ramirez leaves the slider in the zone too often -- now he throws it in counts where batters don't want to swing at junk, and steals strikes. That's how he finally had a normal home run rate and a good year. It seems sustainable, unless batters figure it out and start swinging at those sliders anyway, in which case the projections will be right to show more than a home run per nine innings. But will the price be that high? He should be worth a small investment to see if he can continue to have a normal home run rate, and that double-digit swinging strike rate may even lead to more strikeouts in the future. And more upside. (Eno Sarris)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Erasmo Ramirez is only 25. The Brett Lawrie of pitchers has been on sleeper lists for five years, but he's still in the middle of his peak range. He has the pitches, and last year he put them together in the right order. Nudge the home run rate down and the innings total up, and you'll find a good way to value this young Ray.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Ramirez lost 11 games in 2016... in relief. It's one of those oft-dismissed traditional statistics, but still, that's astounding. It also attests to his heavy usage — he pitched 90.1 innings and recorded at least four outs 35 times — but also his ineffectiveness. One might have thought a full-time move to the bullpen would play up his skill set, yet such a move cultivated the worst strikeout rate of his career. In good news, his ground ball rate spiked as he leaned more heavily on his sinker, thereby weaning off his four-seamer and eradicating his curve. Unfortunately, the sinker isn't much of a strikeout pitch. Ramirez seems interested in improving; further refining his distribution of offerings could revive his lukewarm strikeout rate, for example. But all the optimization in the world may not elevate his ceiling to a  worthwhile level. It would be interesting to see him back in the rotation, given his new focus on killing worms, but an expected over-reliance on contact would be inherently problematic. Entering his age-27 season, Ramirez figures to help only in very deep leagues, and that would only be if he re-entered the rotation. As a reliever, he's worthless. (Alex Chamberlain)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Ramirez took two steps forward and one step back as a full-time reliever for the Rays. He's capable of making changes, but they may not ever manifest in respectable production. Depending on his usage next season, he's at best a very-deep-league flyer.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
            </table>
        </td>

        </td>
    </tr>

    function showMoreSO() {
        //    var panel = document.getElementById('so1');
        //    
        //    if(panel.style.display == 'none')
        //    {
        //        panel.style.display = 'inherit';
        //    }
        //    else
        //    {
        //        panel.style.display = 'inherit';
        //    }

        hideSO('so2');

        var panelo = document.getElementById('so2');

        if (panelo.style.display == 'none') {
            panelo.style.display = 'table-row';
            document.getElementById('soa2').style.fontWeight = 'bold';
        }
        else {
            panelo.style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('soa2').style.fontWeight = 'normal';
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
    // Create the tooltips only on document load
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Notice the use of the each() method to acquire access to each elements attributes
        $('img[tooltip]').each(function () {
            $(this).qtip({
                position: {
                    viewport: $(window),
                    at: "bottomMiddle"
                },
                content: $(this).attr('tooltip'),
                style: {
                    classes: "qtip-dark"
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

    function setAverage(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_average') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setPost(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason_total') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setProj(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_projections_show') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setRegular(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgAltRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_total') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setProjShow(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_projections_hide') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    }

    function setPart(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {

            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }

                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }

        }
    }

    // Create the tooltips only on document load
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Make sure to only match links to wikipedia with a rel tag
        $('a[tipgloss]').each(function () {
            // We make use of the .each() loop to gain access to each element via the "this" keyword...
            $(this).qtip(
		{
		    content: {
		        // Set the text to an image HTML string with the correct src URL to the loading image you want to use
		        text: " ",
		        ajax: {
		            url: $(this).attr('tipgloss') // Use the rel attribute of each element for the url to load
		        }
		    },
		    position: {
		        viewport: $(window),
		        at: "top center",
		        my: "bottom center",
		        effect: false
		    },
		    show: {
		        event: "click mouseenter",
		        solo: true // Only show one tooltip at a time
		    },
		    hide: {
		        event: "click mouseleave",
		        delay: 1000,
		        fixed: true
		    },
		    style: {
		        classes: "qtip-light"
		    }
		})

            // Make sure it doesn't follow the link when we click it
        });
    });
</script>
